# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
ACC = ACC + IMM ^wa1s7q83

2^7 = 7 bits.
/\
 |   ^ byte = 8 bits ^N4qz2unx

2^5 = 5 bits ^ofw43hNV

8K = 2^13 = 13 bits
x8 = byte = 8 bits ^gKlgjtQJ

4 bytes ^xxykyJjH

4 bytes
2 bits ^K7xijP2b

64/4 = 16 => 4 bits6 ^uqzA1tmL

offset ^gXzyn1BW

tag ^UaOAWUlT

tag ^uxmhTF3a

entry # ^MTfRfSzP

101101 | 00
101101 | 01
101101 | 10
101101 | 11 ^ZtsLF8GA

In a DM cache, there is a line size of 4 bytes. Each entry has 4 bits it can hold. 
A specific address is represented by bit offset, but on miss we update the whole line with new values.
* Send all possible values of offset ^VYBs06UK

3x2 = 6
24/6 = 4 caches
   = 6 bytes ^Dr0cnROI

Tag               Cache #    Offset ^AhV9PMUU

Cache 1
11011 ? 
YESh ^hND6G5fZ

Cache 3
10110 ? 
NO ^J07lvw10

0x9B ^a7Jz7QT4

32 bit word
= 32 / 8 = 4 bytes
 ^uDmfsTwW

2x8 = 16 byes
32/16 = 2 = 1 bit ^876mjOBm

Since each has 2 words, 
we need 8 bytes => 3 bits ^2Z1ktfyy

2k = 2^11  ^uTq3ekQA

256 = 2^8 
 = 8 bits wide ^A1zdGkvX

12 bits ^0EATfpiv

011 | 00011001 ^ixCAnnKf

Go from 4|8 address to 3|8 address ^OiOnGShW

011 | 01111010    <-    11 bits ^rSB2yqHd

2^8 ^CCF9Lc7m

16 bits of virtual address
Physical memory is 13 ^r7Ye5Kve

2^13 ^lxQlDXg4

32=2^5 => 5 bits ^dKN8wEng

0x20A4 = Physical Address in memory
0xa9     = Value ^uhSVCanl

Seg fault, presence bit is 0 ^6wBcdMZ6

Page Fault, presence bit in page table is 0 ^Sd2HetW8
